You can disable this feature in the settings page \"Synchronize map with compass (when follow or play is unactive)\". If the option is checked the map rotate with you, otherwise the map is always facing north.\r\n\r\n2) Follow me and draw route on the map. When you stop the function clicking on \"Stop follow me\" , the route will be stored in the device. This way, if you go from point A to point B, you can record the route.\r\n\r\n3) Follow me and don't draw route on the map. In the menu you must click on \"Start follow me / Stop follow me\". This feature is enabled when the option \"Enable track route on map\" in the settings menu is not checked. This way, if you go from point B to point A, you can follow a route on map previously stored and loaded (follow back).\r\n\r\n4) Replay route on the map (a route previously stored in step 2).
